import re
import MeCab
def wakati_sentence(sentence):#文を単語ごとに分ける
    #['明日', 'は', '晴れ', 'か', 'なあ', '\n']
    if sentence in [""[スタンプ]"",""[写真]""]:
        return [sentence,""\n""]
    t = MeCab.Tagger(""-Owakati"")
    parsed_text =t.parse(sentence)
    wordlist = parsed_text.rstrip(""\n"").rstrip("" "").split("" "")+['\n']
    return wordlist
from collections import deque
order = 2#マルコフれんさの階数

def make_sentence_model(raw_talk_text):
    #次のような辞書を作りたい{ (""今日"", ""は"") : [""いい"", ""晴れ"", ""雨"", ・・・] ,(""は"", ""いい"") : [""天気"",""気分"",""天気"", ・・・],(""いい"",""天気""):[""です"",""だ"",""だ"",・・・], ・・・}
    sentence_model = {}
    sentences =[sentence.split(""\t"")[2] for sentence in raw_talk_text.split(""\n"") if len(sentence.split(""\t""))==3 and sentence.split(""\t"")[1]=='松本 華澄']

    print(wakati_sentence(sentences[3]))
    queue = deque([], order)#2個しか入らないリストみたいなもの
    for sentence in sentences:
        queue.append(""[Begin]"")#queue=[""[Begin]"",]
        for markov_value in wakati_sentence(sentence):
            if len(queue) == order:
                markov_key = tuple(queue)      
                if markov_key not in sentence_model:
                    sentence_model[markov_key] = []
                sentence_model[markov_key].append(markov_value)
            queue.append(markov_value)#次の処理に移る。
        
        queue.clear()
    return sentence_model
#%%
def make_reply_model(raw_talk_text):#返信用
    #作成するのは{'ゆく': ['ご飯'], 'な': ['微']}といったような辞書
    sentences =[sentence.split(""\t"") for sentence in raw_talk_text.split(""\n"") if len(sentence.split(""\t""))==3]
    print(""a"",sentences[len(sentences)-1][2]) 
    reply_model={}
    for i in range(len(sentences)-1):
        if sentences[i][1]=='松葉 亮人' and sentences[i+1][1]=='松本 華澄':
            if wakati_sentence(sentences[i][2])[-2] not in reply_model:
                reply_model[wakati_sentence(sentences[i][2])[-2]]=[]
            reply_model[wakati_sentence(sentences[i][2])[-2]].append(wakati_sentence(sentences[i+1][2])[0])
    print(reply_model)

    return reply_model

#%%
import random
def make_sentence(sentence_model={},reply_model={},reply_for="""",max_words = 100): 
    sentence=""""


    

    if reply_for=="""":
        key_candidates = [key for key in sentence_model if key[0] == ""[Begin]""]
        print(key_candidates)       
        if not key_candidates:
            print(""Not find Keyword"")
            return
        markov_key = random.choice(key_candidates)
        queue = deque(list(markov_key), order)
        sentence = """".join(markov_key)
        for _ in range(max_words):
            markov_key = tuple(queue)
            next_word = random.choice(sentence_model[markov_key])
            sentence += next_word
            queue.append(next_word)
            if next_word == ""\n"":
                return sentence
    else:

        key_candidates = [key for key in sentence_model if key[1] == reply_model[wakati_sentence(reply_for)[-2]]]
        return sentence

if __name__ == ""__main__"":
    with open('test.txt', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        raw_talk_text = f.read()
    order = 2

    sentence_model = make_sentence_model(raw_talk_text)
    reply_model=make_reply_model(raw_talk_text)
    print(""sentence_model"",sentence_model)
    print(""reply_model"",reply_model)
    
    
    sentence = make_sentence(sentence_model=sentence_model,reply_model=reply_model)
    print(""sentence"",sentence)
